Went in for tire rotation and oil change because they were having a sale for under $25. Not only did they not rotate my tires but they did not inform me that they would/could not change my tires because they were too worn out until after I called to complain about them not being rotated. When I went in for a following inspection, I was "offered" a fantastic deal on new tires (sarcasm fully intended). So they attempted to up sell me some tires for full price when they couldn't even perform the initial job that I paid them for. Are these guys serious? Scam artists! I was not offered anything for the terrible job and horrendous communication skills they have. Their manager did not even offer any sort of refund for the lack of work done on my vehicle.

I also have doubts about even getting the oil changed, seeing how the dipstick had brownish oil at the bottom. So it seems as though I paid $25 for them to do nothing except lift my car with their hydraulic lift and place it back down.

I did eventually get a full set of new tires from Costco. No hassle and no BS.

I would not recommend getting anything done from these guys. Chances are, you won't even get the work you paid for. Speedee is probably the best place for a quick oil change.

Have I recommended enough places to go besides this scummy company? Any place else is better. ANY PLACE ELSE!!!

<user_id>102751010899109036391< /user_id><name>Jeff Dalton< /name><Date>1538290234862<//Date>< rate>

< review>
It was ok. Got me out of the house. Not much farm to fork. I thought for sure there would be at least a few stands with fresh fruit or vegetables from the farm I could fork.  Mostly beer and wine stands with slim to no selection of beverage. NO random samples of anything. I did in the other hand find one stand that served mixed drinks. At 8$ a Solo cup it seemed to be the reasonable decision to make over the same priced beer. The drinks surprised me. They were amazing. Once again,  I had only a choice of two, the line was very fast. Quik enough to go back a second time. Which was a fantastic way to deal with the large amount of people that were fenced onto a main street. People were very chilled. So it wasn't horrible. The live band was decent and had a good sound considering they were next to the last band on the board. My girlfriend took me. We had a good time together there. Very much dog friendly. That was a plus. We love dog's. Over all it was okay.<//review>

< review>
I'd like to give this company no stars, but I need to give it one star to be able to post this. Appaulling customer service. Bottles arrived to the UK damaged and leaking after being inadequetly packaged. The attitude of Gary when we contacted him about it was appaulling. It took 2 and a half weeks of emails, in which we had to continually chase to get any responce. We never had an apology, and the tone of emails was rude and really disinterested in our situation. Eventually we did manage to get a part refund for the damaged bottles, but it seemed it was more to 'shut us up'. In addition to this we were hit with a bill from Fed Ex Customs and Duty for $150 for bottles which were worth $120 which we didnt expect at all.
